\[
\int{{\frac{2 \, x^{3} - 12 \, x^{2} + 222 \, x - 421}{{\left(3 \, x^{2} - 2 \, x + 3\right)} {\left(x - 8\right)}^{2}}}\;dx} = \answer{{-\frac{19}{12} \, \sqrt{2} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{4} \, \sqrt{2} {\left(3 \, x - 1\right)}\right) - \frac{9}{x - 8} + \frac{1}{3} \, \log\left(3 \, x^{2} - 2 \, x + 3\right)}+C}
\]
\end{problem}}%}

\int{{-\frac{4 \, {\left(x^{3} + 14 \, x^{2} + 26 \, x - 33\right)}}{{\left(3 \, x^{2} + 2 \, x + 3\right)} {\left(x + 6\right)}^{2}}}\;dx} = \answer{{\frac{4}{3} \, \sqrt{2} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{4} \, \sqrt{2} {\left(3 \, x + 1\right)}\right) + \frac{4}{x + 6} - \frac{2}{3} \, \log\left(3 \, x^{2} + 2 \, x + 3\right)}+C}
\]
\end{problem}}%}
